<review>Of course, After's Ice Cream is a chain/franchise business, but its good to know that they are all good and all have good value. The first time I've had their ice cream, I ordered their Mikly Bun - thats an ice-cream sandwich with a donut as the buns. They also have toppings you can add to your order. I recommend getting your scoops of ice cream in a cup because they can really pack it all the way. 3 scoops is actually A LOT of ice cream, and i have a tough time finishing it.

< Review>
I've gone here for both of my puppies for 2 years now. Staff is super friendly and very helpful with any questions. The cost is pay as you go, which I feel is better than being locked into a contract from other veterinary clinics. Other places does monthly pay for unlimited office visits, but if you care for your pet correctly, there shouldn't be a need to pay a contract deal for that service. They also take CareCredit payments, which helps a lot if you are on a budget and can't afford the full payment of the visit right away. CareCredit helps with no interest for 6-12 months; depending on the amount of the visit. They have easy online appointment scheduling for those who doesn't like talking on the phone, and their app sends you reminders of future appointments and prescription refill/appointment recommendations. I was recommended this place by a friend, and I would recommend them to others as well.< /Review>

<Review>My experience with Akaal Pet Hospital  changes every time that I go there.

Pros: They are always very friendly and their prices have always been reasonable.  The wait time when I make an appointment is not long to see the doctors.

Cons:  Every time I call in to refill a prescription they say they have to talk to the doctor.  My pet has been on the same medication for the last 8 years or so.  They always say that they will call me back within the hour but I never get a call back.  I always have to call them back later in the day.  When I do call and they say the doctor has approved it and your prescription is ready to pick up.  When I arrive there my prescription is never ready and I have to wait for them to fill it.  I took my puppy to the vet to get her fixed.  She loved everyone and was very friendly.  Once she got fixed she is afraid of everyone new now.  She also ended up get a UTI which we had to take here there to get medicine to cure it.

I ended up taking my dog to a different vet, Family's Friend Vet, and found out my dog has a birth defect that was very obvious. It was an inverted vulva.  It was very obvious when the vet showed me.  I would have had no idea if the vet didn't show me but I believe that Akaal should have looked when I brought my dog back so recent with another UTI. <gmapID>0x809adf1b6b7eb3c1:0xa94691e1657f496b<//gmapID>< text>
Akaal Pet Hospital saved our cat's life!  We had just adopted our cat Mozzie and made an appointment to have his first check up.  The day before the appointment he wouldn't eat his food and was lethargic, and then we noticed his pupils were different sizes.  At the vet they did tests and determined he had some kind of infection, possibly in his brain!  We had just gotten this cat and he had won our hearts in no time, so this was devastating news.  But, the staff at Akaal were nice, helpful, knowledgeable and professional.  They went right to work to do everything they could for Mozz.  They even took time to collaborate with a vet at UCDavis vet center at our request, no charge.  Our cat had to be on IV antibiotics, pills, ear drops, everything, but their prices were cheap and totally reasonable.  Mozzie went from a poor-to-bad prognosis to pulling through and is today a healthy cat.  They even took time to call several times just to see how he was doing.  Akaal Pet Hospital is awesome and I highly recommend them.</text>

<rate>5</rate>< review>
We have had a unit here for about 1.5 years and it has always been a very clean and helpful storage facility.  We were in preparation to move and sent our mover with a key to the unit to move our stuff to us as we had already left California.  On the morning of the move he lost the key to the unit and had no way to get in.  We were able to work with Myesha to get our unit lock drilled out that same day (she had to do extra leg work to find a district manager that was available) so that they could do the move out the next morning.  They were able to fax the paperwork to our house so that we didn't even have to go anywhere.  The entire process went very smoothly and we were never made to feel like they wouldn't help us.  We really appreciated our stay and will use public storage again in the near future.  We will also recommend it and especially this location to our friends and family.<//review>

You must be looking for Indian food.
Bamm! This is good.
I stopped by for the lunch buffet, having seen their rating of 4.4 stars.
I arrived around 2PM, so the crowd was gone. I AM the crowd.
Started with the lamb curry and curry mushroom. Wow, it made me wanting to try everything on the stand. And it did not disappoint.
You have gotta try the tomato soup.

I was a very appreciative customer at the end of the meal and left happily with a togo box packed with goodies.

<user>101867187599720072916<//user><rating>5</rating><Review>This is the defacto spot for Indian buffet for the S.O. and I. We probably come here 2-3 times a month, but we've been more. The family that runs the place is super friendly and the food is always awesome. The heat and spice of the dishes fluctuates so a dish is never the same twice - there's always something a little different which I think is great since it becomes a conversation piece for us. I typically love the goat curry, chicken makhani, ginger chicken, biryani rice, dal and the cabbage fry but it's all awesome. They hand make the mango lassie's here; we get one every time.

There's lots of Indian food in the area - we feel most at home here.< /Review></record>

<user>105632927775501163881< /user><username>Maria T. Caro< /username><date>1427229286511</date><Rating>5< /Rating>< text>
I moved to Berkeley summer of 2014 & I'm still exploring the area and I love indian cuisine which this town offers ample of ethnic cuisine. So after I googled & read yelp reviews, I called Priya Restaurant to check out their Lunch Buffet. A gentleman answered the phone, answered my questions, kindly & patiently gave me the direction to get there which is only down the street from where I live. Found it easily & as I walked in I was greeted by the older gentleman as well as the person (who after eating, later introduced himself by the name Reddy) I spoke to on the phone, sat me where I wanted to be sitted - by the window. As the older gentleman (forgot his name) pours water on my glass, I mentioned it's my first time at the restaurant, so he escorted me to the food buffet and graciously showed & gave me details of all the food on the carts. Reddy came to my table & introduced himself & spent a couple minutes for a friendly little chat about the restaurant and them  as the family owner. Both gentlemen were very helpful & informative with the food and constantly checked up on me. Food is DELICIOUSLY authentic & EXCELLENT service! I had few dishes that are my first & they are delicious! Will definitely visit again & support this local, excellent & friendly neighborhood eatery.<//text>

<text>Wow. This place is my new favorite Indian food restaurant in the whole bay area. They serve both north AND south Indian cuisine. The have lunch, dinner, and weekend buffets, plus prix fixe dinners. The food is pretty great plus these are some of the best prices I've seen for a buffet or dinner entres anywhere. The buffet is bountiful! About 8 different main dishes, plus lots of sides, super tasty chutneys, desserts, bread, and other add-ons.

Not only is this restaurant great, but the whole block that it's on is amazing; next door is the best middle eastern grocery store I've run across in the bay area, and across the street is a cheese shop (all in a fridge, though, not a counter, so i doubt you can ask for samples), plus a deli meat/charcuterie counter, plus lots of other goodies. And on the other side of Priya is a smaller Rainbow Foods (SF)-like grocery store. Also across the street is Lanesplitters for good beer/pizza, and Acme which is a great local dive bar.<//text><Date>1293155759543</Date></record>

< Text>
WOW!!! Is just not enough!

I have always had this thought that "sandwich is just a sandwich". Literally, Super Tortas re-defined my perception on sandwiches.

The taste is very abundant, it give a spectrum of flavors. The sandwiches are $8~10 and it is in the middle of nowhere - so tourists! You may think it is "not worth the trip" given $10+ uber expense for a single ride (round trip uber expense at least $20+) meaning your fully loaded sandwich cost, assuming you buy just one, is almost $30.

Hold that thought. I would gladly pay $30 for a sandwich if it tastes like THIS.

Had a Cubano and Argentina sandwich - both "off the charts" gooood.< /Text>

<Review>I‚Äôm not saying any one sandwich is better than another, but these are the best Tortas north of the border and I‚Äôve been to Mexico City and it ranks right up there. The real difference is size and construction, but I‚Äôll get more into that later. It‚Äôs not a Mexico City Torta, but it‚Äôs made in that style hence the distrito federal in the name.

Everyone tells you to get the Cubano and it‚Äôs good, but most of those people have never had a real Cubano in Florida and couldn‚Äôt tell you what the difference between that and a Medianoche is. I‚Äôve tried a lot of great sandwiches and part of their glory is simplicity and interplay. The Cubano here is massive, ham, chorizo, egg, 2 cheeses, pork leg, milanesa, avo, mayo, chili, hot dogs and it‚Äôs probably just over a pound and a half. It‚Äôs well constructed and isn‚Äôt messy as long as you leave the wrapper on it while eating, but the egg doesn‚Äôt add anything, the chorizo doesn‚Äôt stand out and you totally lose the Cubano aspect of it all together. Now when you consider this without the name it‚Äôs pretty good, but has way too much going on to compete with famous sandwiches, still very massive with excellent ingredients and well crafted. The telera bread is fresh and I‚Äôm sure they are made larger just for them.

It‚Äôs filling and inexpensive and in my opinion one of the best food trailers in all of LA (should easily be mentioned in the same breath as El Chato). When you watch the tortero making them you realize he‚Äôs got real skill for this stuff. A real specialist. As you watch him make it you may have some regrets on it‚Äôs size. Not some fat sals type stuffed sandwich these ingredients are more thought out and more complimentary. It‚Äôs a sight to see new customers come here their reactions while watching him. They‚Äôve been around for years and are slowly getting acclaim.

Call ahead if you can as long as you don‚Äôt want any crazy customization. They don‚Äôt speak the greatest English so your order may not be right Don‚Äôt take off that wrapper or your going to have a hard time containing all that stuff. The wait can be a little long, but start with the Cubano and then try the other menu items named after different countries/regions like Italy, Holland, Hawaii, Argentina, Spain, etc. They all start the same, same roll, same butter, same mayo, the cheese is always standard gooey quesillo and some have additional cheeses. The fried and breaded beef milanesa in the rusa pairs well with all the liquid ingredients or non meat/cheese parts.

It‚Äôs pretty cool someone did a D.F. stype torta only place. It will really open peoples eyes as I found out myself in my visits to Mexico City was that they have an underappreciated food scene that‚Äôs different from the rest of the country and highly underrepresented here in the states.</Review><pics>None<//pics><response>None<//response><gmap_id>0x80c2c863c44e4407:0xf2c8f9f4aeb6ec5<//gmap_id></record></dataset><record>
